# Data Model: lvm_dap


Multi-extension LVM DAP FITS file containing per-fiber stellar and emission-line analysis products for a single exposure.


## Contents
- [Basic Information](#basic-information)
- [Changelog](#changelog)
- [Example HDUS List](#example-hdus-list)
- [Notes](#notes)
- [Regrets](#regrets)
---

## Basic Information
The file dap-{rspid}-{snlevel}-{expnum}.{daptype}.fits is the standard multi-extension FITS product delivered by the LVM Data Analysis Pipeline for a single reduced frame or row-stacked-spectra exposure. The PRIMARY extension preserves the original input header for traceability, while the remaining table extensions store the position table of each science fiber on the sky, the luminosity-weighted and mass-weighted stellar properties derived from the stellar decomposition, the coefficients of the resolved-stellar-population decomposition, the emission-line measurements from the first and second parametric analyses, the non-parametric emission-line measurements for the blue, red, and infrared spectrograph arms, the instrumental-resolution-corrected velocity dispersions and reduced chi-square values for each analyzed emission line, the average instrumental-resolution correction and chi-square statistics for each line, and the configuration parameters adopted to run the LVM-DAP. Emission-line fluxes are reported in units of 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2 measured in one fiber area, where each fiber area corresponds to 0.2718 arcmin^2; continuum flux densities are reported in units of 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2/Angstrom measured in one fiber area.

### Naming Convention
$LVM_SPECTRO_ANALYSIS/[DRPVER]/[DAPVER]/[TILEGRP]/[TILEID]/[MJD]/[EXPNUM]/dap-[RSPID]-[SNLEVEL]-[EXPNUM]\.[DAPTYPE]\.fits$

### Releases
DR20

### Enviroments
LVM_SPECTRO_ANALYSIS

### Approximate Size
56 MB

### File Type
FITS

### Generated by Product
lvmdap

### Is a VAC
False

### Data Level
2.3.3

  - [HDU11: INFO](#hdu11-info)

## Example HDUS List

### HDU0: PRIMARY
Primary HDU containing no data array and preserving the original header of the analyzed reduced frame for traceability and provenance.

#### HDU Type: IMAGE
#### HDU Size:  0 bytes

### HDU1: PT
Binary table containing the position table that maps each analyzed science fiber to its sky coordinates and identifiers.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  71 KB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU1
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 42 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 1754 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 6 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | PT | extension name |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU1
Name | Type | Unit | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
 | id | char[9] |  | Unique identifier of the analyzed fiber built as EXPNUM.FIBERID. |
 | ra | float64 | degree | Right Ascension of the fiber position on the sky. |
 | dec | float64 | degree | Declination of the fiber position on the sky. |
 | mask | bool |  | Boolean mask flag indicating whether the fiber should be masked in the analysis. |
 | fiberid | int64 |  | Fiber identifier from the original DRP SLITMAP extension. |
 | exposure | int64 |  | Exposure number of the analyzed frame. |



### HDU2: RSP
Binary table containing luminosity-weighted and mass-weighted average stellar parameters derived from the resolved-stellar-population decomposition for each analyzed science fiber.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  426 KB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU2
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 249 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 1754 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 31 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | RSP | extension name |
| COMMENT | (1) MIN_CHISQ |  |
| COMMENT | (2) Teff |  |
| COMMENT | (3) e_Teff |  |
| COMMENT | (4) Log_g |  |
| COMMENT | (5) e_Log_g |  |
| COMMENT | (6) Fe |  |
| COMMENT | (7) e_Fe |  |
| COMMENT | (8) alpha |  |
| COMMENT | (9) e_alpha |  |
| COMMENT | (10) Av |  |
| COMMENT | (11) e_Av |  |
| COMMENT | (12) z |  |
| COMMENT | (13) e_z |  |
| COMMENT | (14) disp |  |
| COMMENT | (15) e_disp |  |
| COMMENT | (16) flux |  |
| COMMENT | (17) redshift |  |
| COMMENT | (18) med_flux |  |
| COMMENT | (19) e_med_flux |  |
| COMMENT | (20) Teff_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (21) e_Teff_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (22) Log_g_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (23) e_Log_g_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (24) Fe_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (25) e_Fe_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (26) alpha_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (27) e_alpha_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (28) sys_vel |  |
| COMMENT | (29) log_ML |  |
| COMMENT | (30) log_Mass |  |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU2
Name | Type | Unit | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
 | id | char[9] |  | Unique identifier of the analyzed fiber built as EXPNUM.FIBERID. |
 | MIN_CHISQ | float64 |  | Minimum chi-square value of the stellar decomposition fit. |
 | Teff | float64 | K | Luminosity-weighted effective temperature of the stellar component. |
 | e_Teff | float64 | K | Uncertainty in the luminosity-weighted effective temperature. |
 | Log_g | float64 | dex | Luminosity-weighted stellar surface gravity log(g). |
 | e_Log_g | float64 | dex | Uncertainty in the luminosity-weighted stellar surface gravity log(g). |
 | Fe | float64 | dex | Luminosity-weighted stellar metallicity [Fe/H]. |
 | e_Fe | float64 | dex | Uncertainty in the luminosity-weighted stellar metallicity [Fe/H]. |
 | alpha | float64 | dex | Luminosity-weighted stellar alpha-element abundance [alpha/Fe]. |
 | e_alpha | float64 | dex | Uncertainty in the luminosity-weighted stellar alpha-element abundance [alpha/Fe]. |
 | Av | float64 | mag | Luminosity-weighted stellar dust attenuation in the V band. |
 | e_Av | float64 | mag | Uncertainty in the luminosity-weighted stellar dust attenuation in the V band. |
 | z | float64 |  | Luminosity-weighted stellar redshift. |
 | e_z | float64 |  | Uncertainty in the luminosity-weighted stellar redshift. |
 | disp | float64 | km/s | Luminosity-weighted stellar velocity dispersion. |
 | e_disp | float64 | km/s | Uncertainty in the luminosity-weighted stellar velocity dispersion. |
 | flux | float64 | 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2/Angstrom | Continuum flux density of the stellar model, measured in one fiber area (0.2718 arcmin^2). |
 | redshift | float64 |  | Adopted stellar redshift used in the stellar decomposition. |
 | med_flux | float64 | 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2/Angstrom | Median continuum flux density, measured in one fiber area (0.2718 arcmin^2). |
 | e_med_flux | float64 | 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2/Angstrom | Uncertainty in the median continuum flux density, measured in one fiber area (0.2718 arcmin^2). |
 | Teff_MW | float64 | K | Mass-weighted effective temperature of the stellar component. |
 | e_Teff_MW | float64 | K | Uncertainty in the mass-weighted effective temperature. |
 | Log_g_MW | float64 | dex | Mass-weighted stellar surface gravity log(g). |
 | e_Log_g_MW | float64 | dex | Uncertainty in the mass-weighted stellar surface gravity log(g). |
 | Fe_MW | float64 | dex | Mass-weighted stellar metallicity [Fe/H]. |
 | e_Fe_MW | float64 | dex | Uncertainty in the mass-weighted stellar metallicity [Fe/H]. |
 | alpha_MW | float64 | dex | Mass-weighted stellar alpha-element abundance [alpha/Fe]. |
 | e_alpha_MW | float64 | dex | Uncertainty in the mass-weighted stellar alpha-element abundance [alpha/Fe]. |
 | sys_vel | float64 | km/s | Systemic stellar velocity. |
 | log_ML | float64 | dex | Logarithm of the stellar mass-to-light ratio. |
 | log_Mass | float64 | log(Msun) | Logarithm of the stellar mass associated with the analyzed fiber. |



### HDU3: COEFFS
Binary table containing the coefficients or weights of the resolved-stellar-population decomposition required to reconstruct the stellar model and associated parameter probability distributions for each fiber.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  18 MB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU3
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 105 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 189432 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 13 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | COEFFS | extension name |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU3
Name | Type | Unit | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
 | id | char[9] |  | Unique identifier of the analyzed fiber built as EXPNUM.FIBERID. |
 | id_fib | int64 |  | Sequential identifier of the analyzed fiber within the RSS or pointing. |
 | rsp | int64 |  | Identifier of the resolved-stellar-population template used in the decomposition. |
 | TEFF | float64 | K | Effective temperature associated with the RSP template. |
 | LOGG | float64 | dex | Surface gravity log(g) associated with the RSP template. |
 | META | float64 | dex | Metallicity [Fe/H] associated with the RSP template. |
 | ALPHAM | float64 | dex | Alpha-element abundance [alpha/Fe] associated with the RSP template. |
 | COEFF | float64 |  | Coefficient or weight assigned to the RSP template in the stellar decomposition. |
 | Min.Coeff | float64 |  | Minimum coefficient assigned or allowed for the RSP template during the fit. |
 | log(M/L) | float64 | dex | Logarithm of the mass-to-light ratio associated with the RSP template. |
 | AV | float64 | mag | Dust attenuation in the V band associated with the RSP template contribution. |
 | N.Coeff | float64 |  | Normalized coefficient of the RSP template in the stellar decomposition. |
 | Err.Coeff | float64 |  | Uncertainty in the coefficient of the RSP template. |



### HDU4: PM_ELINES
Binary table containing the emission-line properties derived from the first parametric fitting analysis after subtraction of the stellar continuum model.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  2 MB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU4
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 84 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 26310 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 10 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | PM_ELINES | extension name |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU4
Name | Type | Unit | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
 | id | char[9] |  | Unique identifier of the analyzed fiber built as EXPNUM.FIBERID. |
 | id_fib | int64 |  | Sequential identifier of the analyzed fiber within the RSS or pointing. |
 | model | char[11] |  | Label identifying the emission-line model fitted in the parametric analysis. |
 | wl | float64 | Angstrom | Rest-frame central wavelength of the fitted emission line. |
 | flux | float64 | 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2 | Emission-line flux from the parametric analysis, measured in one fiber area (0.2718 arcmin^2). |
 | e_flux | float64 | 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2 | Uncertainty in the emission-line flux from the parametric analysis, measured in one fiber area (0.2718 arcmin^2). |
 | disp | float64 | Angstrom | Emission-line velocity dispersion from the parametric analysis, uncorrected for instrumental resolution. |
 | e_disp | float64 | Angstrom | Uncertainty in the emission-line velocity dispersion from the parametric analysis. |
 | vel | float64 | km/s | Emission-line line-of-sight velocity from the parametric analysis. |
 | e_vel | float64 | km/s | Uncertainty in the emission-line line-of-sight velocity from the parametric analysis. |

### HDU6: NP_ELINES_R
Binary table containing the non-parametric emission-line measurements for the red spectrograph arm for each analyzed science fiber.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  3 MB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU6
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 2057 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 1754 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 257 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | NP_ELINES_R | extension name |

### HDU7: NP_ELINES_I
Binary table containing the non-parametric emission-line measurements for the infrared spectrograph arm for each analyzed science fiber.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  7 MB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU7
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 4425 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 1754 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 553 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | NP_ELINES_I | extension name |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU7
Name | Type | Unit | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
 | id | char[9] |  | Unique identifier of the analyzed fiber built as EXPNUM.FIBERID. |

### HDU8: PM_KEL
Binary table containing the emission-line properties derived from the second parametric fitting analysis performed on the gas-pure spectrum after refinement of the stellar model.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  2 MB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU8
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 84 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 36834 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 10 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | PM_KEL | extension name |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU8
Name | Type | Unit | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
 | id | char[9] |  | Unique identifier of the analyzed fiber built as EXPNUM.FIBERID. |
 | id_fib | int64 |  | Sequential identifier of the analyzed fiber within the RSS or pointing. |
 | model | char[11] |  | Label identifying the emission-line model fitted in the parametric analysis. |
 | wl | float64 | Angstrom | Rest-frame central wavelength of the fitted emission line. |
 | flux | float64 | 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2 | Emission-line flux from the parametric analysis, measured in one fiber area (0.2718 arcmin^2). |
 | e_flux | float64 | 10^-16 erg/s/cm^2 | Uncertainty in the emission-line flux from the parametric analysis, measured in one fiber area (0.2718 arcmin^2). |
 | disp | float64 | Angstrom | Emission-line velocity dispersion from the parametric analysis, uncorrected for instrumental resolution. |
 | e_disp | float64 | Angstrom | Uncertainty in the emission-line velocity dispersion from the parametric analysis. |
 | vel | float64 | km/s | Emission-line line-of-sight velocity from the parametric analysis. |
 | e_vel | float64 | km/s | Uncertainty in the emission-line line-of-sight velocity from the parametric analysis. |



### HDU9: ELINES_SIGMA_CHI
Binary table containing instrumental-resolution-corrected emission-line velocity dispersions in km/s together with reduced chi-square statistics for the stellar and emission-line fits for each analyzed science fiber.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  6 MB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU9
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 3953 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 1754 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 739 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | ELINES_SIGMA_CHI | extension name |
| COMMENT | (1) MIN_CHISQ |  |
| COMMENT | (2) Teff |  |
| COMMENT | (3) e_Teff |  |
| COMMENT | (4) Log_g |  |
| COMMENT | (5) e_Log_g |  |
| COMMENT | (6) Fe |  |
| COMMENT | (7) e_Fe |  |
| COMMENT | (8) alpha |  |
| COMMENT | (9) e_alpha |  |
| COMMENT | (10) Av |  |
| COMMENT | (11) e_Av |  |
| COMMENT | (12) z |  |
| COMMENT | (13) e_z |  |
| COMMENT | (14) disp |  |
| COMMENT | (15) e_disp |  |
| COMMENT | (16) flux |  |
| COMMENT | (17) redshift |  |
| COMMENT | (18) med_flux |  |
| COMMENT | (19) e_med_flux |  |
| COMMENT | (20) Teff_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (21) e_Teff_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (22) Log_g_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (23) e_Log_g_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (24) Fe_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (25) e_Fe_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (26) alpha_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (27) e_alpha_MW |  |
| COMMENT | (28) sys_vel |  |
| COMMENT | (29) log_ML |  |
| COMMENT | (30) log_Mass |  |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU9

### HDU10: ELINES_CHI2_AVG
Binary table containing the per-line instrumental-resolution correction information and average reduced chi-square statistics for the original, first parametric, second parametric, and non-parametric emission-line analyses.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  1 MB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU10
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 7076 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 245 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 8 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | ELINES_CHI2_AVG | extension name |
| TDIM3 | (1754) |  |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU10
Name | Type | Unit | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
 | name | char[16] |  | Name of the analyzed emission line. |
 | wave | float64 | Angstrom | Rest-frame wavelength of the analyzed emission line. |
 | inst_disp | float32[1754] | Angstrom | Array of instrumental-dispersion corrections applied to the analyzed emission line for all fibers. |
 | X_sq | float64 |  | Reduced chi-square statistic associated with the instrumental-resolution correction for the analyzed emission line. |
 | fr | float32 |  | Average instrumental-resolution correction factor applied to the analyzed emission line. |
 | X_sq_avg_org | float64 |  | Average reduced chi-square of the original-spectrum fit for the analyzed emission line. |
 | X_sq_avg_pek | float64 |  | Average reduced chi-square of the second parametric fit for the analyzed emission line. |
 | X_sq_avg_np | float64 |  | Average reduced chi-square of the non-parametric fit for the analyzed emission line. |



### HDU11: INFO
Binary table containing the configuration parameters and values adopted to run the LVM-DAP for the current analysis.

#### HDU Type: BINARY TABLE
#### HDU Size:  5 KB

##### Header Table Caption for HDU11
Key | Value | Comment | |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| XTENSION | BINTABLE | binary table extension |
| BITPIX | 8 | array data type |
| NAXIS | 2 | number of array dimensions |
| NAXIS1 | 106 | length of dimension 1 |
| NAXIS2 | 50 | length of dimension 2 |
| PCOUNT | 0 | number of group parameters |
| GCOUNT | 1 | number of groups |
| TFIELDS | 2 | number of table fields |
| EXTNAME | INFO | extension name |

##### Binary Table Caption for HDU11
Name | Type | Unit | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
 | param | char[24] |  | Name of the configuration parameter adopted to run the LVM-DAP analysis. |
 | value | char[82] |  | Value assigned to the corresponding configuration parameter in the current run. |
